We will let you take shifts to go in a watch, but cannot promise a seat.You may end up standing in the back. Please note, you will stay busy! It is our best intention to let you see some of the show and we will try our best to allow you time for a break. So plan on working the begining, intermission, and end of the concert.\r\n\r\nQ: How important is it that I arrivefrom 5:00PM?\r\nA: Very important! Volunteers will be checked in and escorted to merchandise promtly at 5:00PM. There is a mandatory training soon after. Please allow time for parking and getting to the entrance.\r\n\r\nQ: How late will I need to stay?\r\nA: We will need you until approximately 30 minutes after the concert finishes, this may be as late as10:30PM. So be prepared to stay and help load out.\r\n\r\nQ: Why is it important that I stay up to 30 minutes after the concert?\r\nA: It's very important that you stay up to 30 minutes after the concert is over. When the concert finishes people tend to stop by the booths with questions or last minute purchases. The road reps also need help packing out and it's much harder if they are left alone to do all of this. We understand it gets late, however, we really need you to stay the whole time.\r\n\r\nQ: How will I know where to go? It is our best intention to let you see some of the show and we will try our best to allow you time for a break. So plan on working the begining, intermission, and end of the concert.\r\n\r\nQ: How important is it that I arrivefrom 5:00PM?\r\nA: Very important! Volunteers will be checked in and escorted to merchandise promtly at 5:00PM. There is a mandatory training soon after. Please allow time for parking and getting to the entrance.\r\n\r\nQ: How late will I need to stay?\r\nA: We will need you until approximately 30 minutes after the concert finishes, this may be as late as10:30PM. So be prepared to stay and help load out.\r\n\r\nQ: Why is it important that I stay up to 30 minutes after the concert?\r\nA: It's very important that you stay up to 30 minutes after the concert is over. When the concert finishes people tend to stop by the booths with questions or last minute purchases. The road reps also need help packing out and it's much harder if they are left alone to do all of this. We understand it gets late, however, we really need you to stay the whole time.\r\n\r\nQ: How will I know where to go? Or who is my contact?\r\nA: Once you sign up, we will be sending you a couple confirmation emails with all the information you need. We will let you take shifts to go in and watch, but cannot promise a seat.You may end up standing in the back. Please note, you will stay busy! It is our best intention to let you see some of the show and we will try our best to allow you time for a break. So plan on working the begining, intermission, and end of the concert.\r\n\r\nQ: How important is it that I arrive at 4:00PM?\r\nA: Very important!Volunteers will be checked in and escorted to tables for training promptly at 4:00PM.Please allow time for parking and finding the volunteer entrance.\r\n\r\nQ: How late will I need to stay and why?\r\nA: We will need you to stay at least 30 minutes after the concert finishes, this may be as late as 11:00PM. So be prepared to stay and help pack up. When the concert finishes people tend to stop by the booths with questions or last minute purchases.\r\n\r\nQ: How will I know where to go? Or who is my contact?\r\nA: Once you sign up, we will be sending you a couple confirmation emails with all the information you need.
